and if i get too close to him , he gets scared just like any other creature .	如果我太接近他 , 他就會害怕就像其他生物一樣 。
so in a lot of ways , romo is like a pet that has a mind of his own .	所以 , 在很多方面 , 羅馬就像一隻寵物一樣 , 羅馬就像一隻寵物一樣 。
thanks , little guy .	謝謝 , 小傢伙 。
and if i want to explore the world uhoh , romo's tired if i want to explore the world with romo , i can actually connect him from any other ios device .	如果我想要探索世界 , 羅馬比我想要探究世界 , 羅馬很想探索這個世界 , 我真的可以把他從任何其他ios裝置連結起來 。
so here's the ipad .	這是ipad 。
and romo will actually stream video to this device .	羅馬會把影片帶到這個裝置 。

now this is a free app on the app store , so if any of you guys had this app on your phones , we could literally right now share control of the robot and play games together .	這是一個免費應用程式的應用程式 , 如果你們有任何人在手機上使用這個應用程式 , 那麼 , 我們現在可以在你的手機上使用這個應用程式 , 所以 , 如果你們有任何人在手機上使用手機 , 我們就可以真正地控制機器人和玩遊戲 。
so i'll show you really quickly , romo actually he's streaming video , so you can see me and the entire ted audience .	接下來我會播放一段影片 , 所以你可以看見我和ted觀眾 。

and in the same way that you scroll through content on an ipad , i can actually adjust the angle of the camera on the device .	同樣地 , 在ipad上 , 我可以調整一下攝影機的角度來調整這個角度 。
so there are all of you through romo's eyes .	所以 , 在羅姆的眼睛中 , 你都看到了romo的眼睛 。
and finally , because romo is an extension of me , i can express myself through his emotions .	最後 , 因為romo是我的延伸 , 我可以表達自己自己透過他的情緒 。
so i can go in and i can say let's make romo excited .	所以 , 我可以說 , 我可以說 , 讓我們讓romo興奮 。
but the most important thing about romo is that we wanted to create something that was literally completely intuitive .	但關於romo最重要的事情是我們想要創造出完全完全直覺的東西 。
you do not have to teach someone how to drive romo .	你不需要教導別人如何駕駛romo 。
in fact , who would like to drive a robot ?	事實上 , 誰會喜歡駕駛機器人 ?
thank you , scott .	謝謝 , 史考特 。
and even cooler , you actually don't have to be in the same geographic location as the robot to control him .	更酷的是 , 你其實不需要在同一個地理位置 , 例如機器人控制他 。
so he actually streams twoway audio and video between any two smart devices .	所以他實際上在兩個聰明裝置之間傳播兩種智慧設備 。
so you can log in through the browser , and it's kind of like skype on wheels .	所以你可以用瀏覽器 , 它就像在輪子的天花板 。
so we were talking before about telepresence , and this is a really cool example .	所以 , 我們在談話題時 , 其實是很酷的例子 。
you can imagine an eightyearold girl , for example , who has an iphone , and her mom buys her a robot .	你可以想像一個八歲的女孩 , 例如有iphone , 她媽媽買她的機器人 。
that girl can take her iphone , put it on the robot , send an email to grandma , who lives on the other side of the country .	那個女孩可以拿她的iphone , 把它放在機器人上 , 寄電子郵件給祖母 , 住在國家的另一邊 。
grandma can log into that robot and play hideandgoseek with her granddaughter for fifteen minutes every single night , when otherwise she might only be able to get to see her granddaughter once or twice a year .	祖母可以用她的孫女去看她的孫女 , 每天晚上兩次 , 只能看到她的孫女 , 或兩次 。
so those are a couple of the really cool things that romo can do today .	所以 , 這些是現今羅馬最酷的事情之一 。
but i just want to finish by talking about something that we're working on in the future .	最後 , 我想談談我們在未來所做的事 。
this is actually something that one of our engineers , dom , built in a weekend .	這是我們的工程師 , 一個星期末 。
it's built on top of a google open framework called blockly .	它在google開放的架構上 , 叫做 「 區塊 」 。
this allows you to drag and drop these blocks of semantic code and create any behavior for this robot you want .	這使得你要把石塊拆開 , 讓你想要 , 把這些零件混合在一起 , 創造出任何行為 。
you do not have to know how to code to create a behavior for romo .	你不需要知道如何編碼如何編碼為romo創造一個行為 。
and you can actually simulate that behavior in the browser , which is what you see romo doing on the left .	你可以實際模擬這種行為在瀏覽器中可以看到romo在左邊做的
and then if you have something you like , you can download it onto your robot and execute it in real life , run the program in real life .	如果你有一些你喜歡的東西 , 你可以下載到你的機器人上 , 去執行現實生活的程式 。
and then if you have something you're proud of , you can share it with every other person who owns a robot in the world .	如果你有一些你很驕傲的事 , 你可以和其他人分享它 , 在世界各地的機器人 。
so all of these wifi–enabled robots actually learn from each other .	所以 , 所有的這些線性機器人都能從彼此學習 。
the reason we're so focused on building robots that everyone can train is that we think the most compelling use cases in personal robotics are personal .	我們非常專注於建造機器人的每一個人 , 每個人都能訓練 , 是我們認為最有用的個人機器人是個人機械的 。
they change from person to person .	他們從人身上改變 。
so we think that if you're going to have a robot in your home , that robot ought to be a manifestation of your own imagination .	所以 , 我們認為如果你在你的家裡有一個機器人 , 機器人應該是你自己的想像力 。
so i wish that i could tell you what the future of personal robotics looks like .	所以 , 我希望我能告訴你未來的個人機器人的樣子 。
to be honest , i have no idea .	老實說 , 我不知道 。
but what we do know is that it isn't 10 years or 10 billion dollars or a large humanoid robot away .	但我們知道的 , 不是10億美金或大型人工機器人 。
the future of personal robotics is happening today , and it's going to depend on small , agile robots like romo and the creativity of people like yourselves .	個人機器人的未來 , 將會依賴小型的機器人 , 像是romo和創造力的人 , 像你自己一樣 。
so we can't wait to get you all robots , and we can't wait to see what you build .	所以 , 我們等不及等待你看到你建造的東西 。
author and activist isabel allende discusses women , creativity , the definition of feminism and , of course , passion in this talk .	作者和行動主義者 , 對於女性主義的定義 , 當然 , 熱情在這個演說中 。
entertainment , global issues , love , parenting , storytelling , women , world cultures	娛樂、全球性議題、愛、養育、故事、女人、世界文化 。
isabel allende tells tales of passion	伊莎貝爾•艾爾維爾說出了關於熱情的訊息 。
thank you so much . it's really scary to be here among the smartest of the smart .	非常謝謝你 , 非常可怕 , 來到這裡 , 非常可怕 。
i'm here to tell you a few tales of passion .	我在這裡要告訴各位一些關於熱情的熱情 。
there's a jewish saying that i love .	有一個猶太人說我愛 。
what is truer than truth ? answer: the story .	什麼比真相呢 ? 答案是:故事 。
i'm a storyteller . i want to convey something that is truer than truth about our common humanity .	我是說故事者 , 我想要傳達出我們常常人類的真相 。
all stories interest me , and some haunt me until i end up writing them .	所有故事都對我有興趣 , 直到我最後寫了它們 。
certain themes keep coming up: justice , loyalty , violence , death , political and social issues , freedom .	有些人會繼續出現:正義、忠誠、暴力、死亡、政治和社會議題 , 自由 。
i'm aware of the mystery around us , so i write about coincidences , premonitions , emotions , dreams , the power of nature , magic .	我意識到我們周遭的神秘 , 所以我寫了關於巧合、情緒、夢想、魔法的力量 。
in the last 20 years i have published a few books , but i have lived in anonymity until february of 2006 , when i carried the olympic flag in the winter olympics in italy .	在過去20年 , 我發表了幾本書 , 但在2006年 , 我在義大利的奧林匹克州贏家奧運會發表了幾本書 。
that made me a celebrity . now people recognize me in macy's , and my grandchildren think that i'm cool .	這使我成為了名人 。 現在人們認識我在馬西 , 我的孫子認為我很酷 。
allow me to tell you about my four minutes of fame .	讓我告訴你們關於我四分鐘的信息 。
one of the organizers of the olympic ceremony , of the opening ceremony , called me and said that i had been selected to be one of the flagbearers .	奧林匹克法典禮儀的其中一位參選者 , 叫做我被選為是旗幟之一 。
i replied that surely this was a case of mistaken identity because i'm as far as you can get from being an athlete .	我複製說 , 這是錯誤的認知 , 因為我身分很遠 , 可以從運動員身上得到運動 。
actually , i wasn't even sure that i could go around the stadium without a walker .	實際上 , 我甚至不確定我可以在座位上游泳 , 沒有人走路 。
i was told that this was no laughing matter .	我被告知這不是笑聲 。
this would be the first time that only women would carry the olympic flag .	這是第一次 , 只有女性會帶著奧運旗幟 。
five women , representing five continents , and three olympic gold medal winners .	五個女性 , 代表五個大陸 , 還有三位奧林匹克贏家 。
my first question was , naturally , what was i going to wear ?	我的第一個問題是 , 天然 , 我會穿什麼 ?
a uniform , she said , and asked for my measurements .	一個制服 , 她說 , 請求我的衡量 。
i had a vision of myself in a fluffy anorak , looking like the michelin man .	我對我自己有一個視覺 , 看起來像米契林人 。
by the middle of february , i found myself in turin , where enthusiastic crowds cheered when any of the 80 olympic teams was in the street .	在二月時 , 我發現我自己在街頭 , 那裡有熱情的群眾 , 每八十個奧林匹克在街上 , 都在街上遊行 。
those athletes had sacrificed everything to compete in the games .	那些運動員已經犧牲了一切在遊戲中競爭 。
they all deserved to win , but there's the element of luck .	他們都應該贏 , 但有幸運的運算 。
a speck of snow , an inch of ice , the force of the wind , can determine the result of a race or a game .	一片冰層的風力 , 風的力量 , 可以決定結果 , 或比賽的力量 。
however , what matters most more than training or luck is the heart .	然而 , 最重要的訓練或運氣是心臟 。
only a fearless and determined heart will get the gold medal .	只有無懼且堅定的心臟會得到金牌 。
it is all about passion .	重點是關於熱情 。
the streets of turin were covered with red posters announcing the slogan of the olympics .	土耳其覆蓋著紅色海報 , 宣佈了奧林匹克的圖表 。
passion lives here . isn't it always true ?	熱情生活在這裡 , 不是總是真的嗎 ?
heart is what drives us and determines our fate .	心臟是驅動我們並決定我們的命運 。
that is what i need for my characters in my books: a passionate heart .	這就是我在書中所需要的:熱情心臟 。
i need mavericks , dissidents , adventurers , outsiders and rebels , who ask questions , bend the rules and take risks .	我需要mavericks、外國人、外叛者、外觀者、外叛者、外叛者、外叛者、外叛者、外叛者、外叛者、外叛者、外叛者、外叛者、外叛者、外叛者、外叛者、外叛者 , 會問問題:
people like all of you in this room .	像在座的各位一樣 。
nice people with common sense do not make interesting characters .	很有趣的人 , 都不會做出有趣的角色 。
they only make good former spouses .	牠們只會做出好前的配偶 。
in the green room of the stadium , i met the other flag bearers: three athletes , and the actresses susan sarandon and sophia loren .	在溫室 , 我遇見了其他旗幟:三項運動員 , 和蘇菲亞•洛倫 。
also , two women with passionate hearts: wangari maathai , the nobel prizewinner from kenya who has planted 30 million trees . and by doing so , she has changed the soil , the weather , in some places in africa , and of course the economic conditions in many villages .	另外 , 兩個女人有熱情心臟:wangarimaathai , 來自肯亞的諾貝爾獎得主 , 她改變了土壤 , 天氣 , 有些地方 , 在非洲 , 也有許多村落的經濟條件 。
and somaly mam , a cambodian activist who fights passionately against child prostitution .	一位柬埔寨積極主義者對抗孩童妓女非常有熱情
when she was 14 years old , her grandfather sold her to a brothel .	當她十四歲時 , 她的祖父賣了她到哥哥 。
she told us of little girls raped by men who believe that having sex with a very young virgin will cure them from aids .	她告訴我們小女孩被男人強暴 , 她們會從愛滋病中獲得愛滋病 。
and of brothels where children are forced to receive five , 15 clients per day , and if they rebel , they are tortured with electricity .	孩子們被迫接受五十五個客戶 , 如果他們叛軍 , 他們就會被迫接收到五個客戶 。
in the green room i received my uniform .	在綠色房間裡我接受了我的制服 。
it was not the kind of outfit that i normally wear , but it was far from the michelin man suit that i had anticipated . not bad , really .	其實不是壞事 , 我通常穿著它 , 但它是來自我很熟悉的英格蘭人 , 不錯 。 不錯 。
i looked like a refrigerator .	我看起來像是冰箱 。
but so did most of the flagbearers , except sophia loren , the universal symbol of beauty and passion .	但 , 大部分的旗幟都是美麗和熱情的象徵 。
sophia is over 70 and she looks great .	蘇菲亞大約七十歲 , 她看起來很棒 。
she's sexy , slim and tall , with a deep tan .	她是性愛、脆弱、和高塔 。
now , how can you have a deep tan and have no wrinkles ?	那麼 , 你要如何有一個深度的坦尚和沒有皺紋呢 ?
when asked in a tv interview , " how could she look so good ? "	當電視訪問時問: 「 她怎麼看得這麼好 ? 」
she replied , " posture . my back is always straight , and i don't make old people's noises . "	她回答: 「 姿勢 , 我沒有老人的噪音 。 」
so , there you have some free advice from one of the most beautiful women on earth .	所以 , 你有一些自由建議 , 來自世界上最美麗的女性之一 。
no grunting , no coughing , no wheezing , no talking to yourselves , no farting .	不開頭 , 不打招呼 , 沒有打算 , 不用煩惱 , 沒人談話 , 沒有人 。
well , she didn't say that exactly .	嗯 , 她不這麼說 。
at some point around midnight , we were summoned to the wings of the stadium , and the loudspeakers announced the olympic flag , and the music started by the way , the same music that starts here , the aida march .	大約在午夜 , 我們被告示了奧林匹克的聲響 , 音樂開始從這裡 , 阿迪達遊行 。
sophia loren was right in front of me she's a foot taller than i am , not counting the poofy hair .	蘇菲亞•洛倫在我面前 , 比我還高 , 不在我面前 , 她是腳高的比我 , 而不是在我面前 。
she walked elegantly , like a giraffe on the african savannah , holding the flag on her shoulder . i jogged behind on my tiptoes holding the flag on my extended arm , so that my head was actually under the damn flag .	她好像一名穿著衣服的旗幟 , 穿著旗幟穿著她的肩膀 , 穿著旗幟穿著她的肩膀 , 直到她肩膀上 , 拿著旗子的旗子 , 直到她肩膀上 。
all the cameras were , of course , on sophia .	所有的攝影機都在蘇菲亞 。
that was fortunate for me , because in most press photos i appear too , although often between sophia's legs .	我很幸運 , 因為在大部分的媒體照片中 , 我也看到了 , 儘管大部分的照片都很幸運 。
a place where most men would love to be .	大部分的人都喜歡這個地方 。
the best four minutes of my entire life were those in the olympic stadium .	我整個人生中最好的四分鐘 , 就是在奧林匹克運動場 。
my husband is offended when i say this although i have explained to him that what we do in private usually takes less than four minutes so he shouldn't take it personally .	我的丈夫正當我向他說 , 雖然我告訴他 , 我們在私人身上做的事 , 通常只有4分鐘 , 所以他不應該去私人 。
i have all the press clippings of those four magnificent minutes , because i don't want to forget them when old age destroys my brain cells .	我有這四個美好的時刻 , 因為我不想忘記他們當老年齡毀了我的大腦細胞 。
i want to carry in my heart forever the key word of the olympics passion .	我想要帶著我的心跳 , 最主要的奧林匹克熱情 。
so here's a tale of passion .	這裡是熱情的熱情
the year is 1998 , the place is a prison camp for tutsi refugees in congo .	那是1998年 , 一個囚犯在剛果的監獄營營 。
by the way , 80 percent of all refugees and displaced people in the world are women and girls .	順道一提 , 世界上80%的難民和殘疾人士都是女性和女孩 。
we can call this place in congo a death camp , because those who are not killed will die of disease or starvation .	我們可以稱之為 「 死亡營地 」 , 因為那些沒有殺死的人 , 會被殺死 , 或飢餓 。
the protagonists of this story are a young woman , rose mapendo , and her children .	這個故事的主角是一位年輕女子 , 蘿絲 , 和她的孩子 。
she's pregnant and a widow .	她懷孕和寡婦 。
soldiers have forced her to watch as her husband was tortured and killed .	士兵們強迫她去看她的丈夫被折磨和殺害 。
somehow she manages to keep her seven children alive , and a few months later , she gives birth to premature twins .	不知怎麼 , 她會讓她的七個孩子活下來 , 幾個月後 , 她出生前就產卵雙胞胎 。
two tiny little boys .	兩個小男孩 。
she cuts the umbilical cord with a stick , and ties it with her own hair .	她切割腫瘤的頭髮 , 用她的頭髮來做 。
she names the twins after the camp's commanders to gain their favor , and feeds them with black tea because her milk cannot sustain them .	她稱之為雙胞胎 , 用黑茶茶 , 因為她的牛奶無法保持他們 。
when the soldiers burst in her cell to rape her oldest daughter , she grabs hold of her and refuses to let go , even when they hold a gun to her head .	當士兵把槍擊到她的頭上 , 她抓住了她和拒絕的女兒 , 抓住她 , 抓住她 , 她抓住她 , 她抓住她 , 她抓住她 , 她抓住她 , 她抓住她 , 她抓住她 。
somehow , the family survives for 16 months , and then , by extraordinary luck , and the passionate heart of a young american man , sasha chanoff , who manages to put her in a u . s . rescue plane , rose mapendo and her nine children end up in phoenix , arizona , where they're now living and thriving .	不管怎樣 , 這家生存活了十六個月 , 後來 , 一個美國人的心臟 , 亞利桑那州 , 亞利桑那州的心臟 , 讓她成為美國人的心臟 , 亞利桑那州 , 她的心臟 , 為十六個月 , 創造了一份美麗的心情 , 讓她成為美國人的心臟 , 亞利桑納 , 在那裡 , 他們的生活和茁壯 。
mapendo , in swahili , means great love .	地圖西里的地圖西里 , 代表偉大的愛情 。
the protagonists of my books are strong and passionate women like rose mapendo .	我的書籍的主題是強烈且熱情的女性 , 比如蘿絲•地圖 。
i don't make them up . there's no need for that .	我不會把它們放出來 , 沒有需要 。
i look around and i see them everywhere .	我看著周圍 , 看到他們 。
i have worked with women and for women all my life .	我和女人和女人一起工作 , 為女性和我的生活 。
i know them well .	我知道他們很好 。
i was born in ancient times , at the end of the world , in a patriarchal catholic and conservative family .	我出生在古老的時代 , 在世界各地 , 在一個父教教室和保守家庭 。
no wonder that by age five i was a raging feminist although the term had not reached chile yet , so nobody knew what the heck was wrong with me .	不想五歲時 , 我是個老化女權主義者雖然這個名字還不完美 , 所以沒有人知道我是怎麼搞的 。
i would soon find out that there was a high price to pay for my freedom , and for questioning the patriarchy .	我很快就發現 , 有一個高價錢 , 為我的自由提供自由 , 並且為財政策劃 。
but i was happy to pay it , because for every blow that i received , i was able to deliver two .	但我很高興能付出這一切 , 因為在我收到的每一塊 , 我都能得到兩份 。
once , when my daughter paula was in her twenties , she said to me that feminism was dated , that i should move on .	一旦 , 當我女兒保羅拉在她的二十歲時 , 她告訴我 , 女兒保羅拉在她身上 , 我應該要搬動 。
we had a memorable fight . feminism is dated ?	我們有了不可思議的戰爭 , 女權主義是約會的 ?
yes , for privileged women like my daughter and all of us here today , but not for most of our sisters in the rest of the world who are still forced into premature marriage , prostitution , forced labor they have children that they don't want or they cannot feed .	是的 , 像我女兒和我們今天的女兒和所有人 , 但不是在世界上大部分的姊妹們 , 仍然被迫害怕她們的孩子 , 她們不想要或無法餵飽 。
they have no control over their bodies or their lives .	他們沒有控制自己的身體或生命 。
they have no education and no freedom .	他們沒有教育 , 也沒有自由 。
they are raped , beaten up and sometimes killed with impunity .	他們被強暴、被逮捕 , 有時被殺害 。
for most western young women of today , being called a feminist is an insult .	現今大部分西方的年輕女性主義者是一種侮辱 。
feminism has never been sexy , but let me assure you that it never stopped me from flirting , and i have seldom suffered from lack of men .	女性主義從來沒有人過性 , 但我讓我保證你從來沒有過過性感 , 讓我保證 , 從來沒有過過性感 , 讓我保證她從來沒有過過性感 , 讓我保證你從來沒有過過性感 , 讓我保證從未有過性感 。
feminism is not dead , by no means .	女性主義不是死的 , 沒有意義 。
it has evolved . if you don't like the term , change it , for goddess' sake .	它已經進化了 。 如果你不喜歡這個詞 , 改變它 , 為上帝的命運 。
call it aphrodite , or venus , or bimbo , or whatever you want ; the name doesn't matter , as long as we understand what it is about , and we support it .	稱它為 「 愛滋病 」 , 或 「 不論 」 的名字 , 不論你想要什麼 , 都不重要 , 只要我們了解它是什麼 , 我們支持它 。
so here's another tale of passion , and this is a sad one .	這裡還有另一個關於熱情的故事 , 這是一個悲傷 。
the place is a small women's clinic in a village in bangladesh .	在孟加拉的一個村莊 , 有一個小婦女診所 。
the year is 2005 .	那是2005年 。
jenny is a young american dental hygienist who has gone to the clinic as a volunteer during her threeweek vacation .	珍妮是一位年輕的美國牙醫牙醫師 , 在她的三週假期時 , 要去診所當志工 。
she's prepared to clean teeth , but when she gets there , she finds out that there are no doctors , no dentists , and the clinic is just a hut full of flies .	她準備好清潔牙齒 , 但當她走到那裡 , 她發現沒有醫生 , 沒有醫生 , 沒有醫生 , 沒有醫生 , 沒有醫生 , 沒有醫生 , 沒有醫師 。
outside , there is a line of women who have waited several hours to be treated .	外面有一群婦女 , 等待了幾小時才能被治療 。
the first patient is in excruciating pain because she has several rotten molars .	第一位患者是非常痛苦的因為她有幾種羅特的母親
jenny realizes that the only solution is to pull out the bad teeth .	珍妮意識到唯一的解決方法就是拿出最好的牙齒 。
she's not licensed for that ; she has never done it .	她從來沒有做過這樣的事 , 她從來沒有做過 。
she risks a lot and she's terrified .	她的風險很大 , 她很害怕 。
she doesn't even have the proper instruments , but fortunately she has brought some novocaine .	她甚至沒有適合的儀器 , 但幸運的是她帶了一些鼻子 。
jenny has a brave and passionate heart .	珍妮有勇氣和熱情的心 。
she murmurs a prayer and she goes ahead with the operation .	她打電話給禱告 , 她向前禱告 。
at the end , the relieved patient kisses her hands .	最後 , 病人親吻她的手 。
that day the hygienist pulls out many more teeth .	那天那天 , 衛生部長出了很多牙齒 。
the next morning , when she comes again to the socalled clinic , her first patient is waiting for her with her husband .	第二天早上 , 她的第一個病人在等待她的丈夫時 , 她的第一個病人在等待她 。
the woman's face looks like a watermelon .	女人的臉看起來就像是水龍 。
it is so swollen that you can't even see the eyes .	很腫瘤 , 你甚至看不到眼睛 。
the husband , furious , threatens to kill the american .	丈夫、憤怒、威脅要殺死美國人 。
jenny is horrified at what she has done , but then the translator explains that the patient's condition has nothing to do with the operation .	珍妮在她所做的事情上很嚇人 , 但後來翻譯解釋病人的狀況和手術沒有關係 。
the day before , her husband beat her up because she was not home in time to prepare dinner for him .	第一天 , 她的丈夫打敗她 , 因為她沒家去準備晚餐 。
millions of women live like this today .	今天有數百萬的女性像這樣 。
they are the poorest of the poor .	他們是窮人最貧窮的人 。
although women do twothirds of the world's labor , they own less than one percent of the world's assets .	儘管女性有三分之二的勞動力 , 但世界上的勞動力少於百分之三十 。
they are paid less than men for the same work if they're paid at all , and they remain vulnerable because they have no economic independence , and they are constantly threatened by exploitation , violence and abuse .	他們比男性一樣工作 , 只要他們付錢 , 他們就被剝削、暴力和虐待 , 被剝削、暴力和虐待 。
it is a fact that giving women education , work , the ability to control their own income , inherit and own property , benefits the society .	事實是 , 提供女性教育、工作能力 , 控制自己的收入、遺產、以及自己的財產 , 來控制自己的收入、財產、以及自己的財產 , 來控制自己的收入 , 和自己的財產 , 來控制自己的收入 , 和自己的財產 。
if a woman is empowered , her children and her family will be better off .	如果女性有權力 , 她的孩子和家人會更好 。
if families prosper , the village prospers , and eventually so does the whole country .	如果家庭繁榮 , 村莊繁榮 , 最終 , 整個國家都會成功 。
wangari maathai goes to a village in kenya .	孟加拉的村落在肯亞的村落 。
she talks with the women and explains that the land is barren because they have cut and sold the trees .	她和婦女談話 , 說 , 土地是荒野的 , 因為他們砍伐了樹木 。
she gets the women to plant new trees and water them , drop by drop .	她讓女性植物新的樹木和水 , 滴滴 。
in a matter of five or six years , they have a forest , the soil is enriched , and the village is saved .	在五或六年之內 , 他們有森林 , 土壤被拯救了 。
the poorest and most backward societies are always those that put women down .	最貧窮和最貧窮的最貧窮最貧窮最貧窮的人通常會把女性放下來 。
yet this obvious truth is ignored by governments and also by philanthropy .	但顯然的事實是忽略政府和慈善事業 。
for every dollar given to a women's program , 20 dollars are given to men's programs .	每一塊錢給予男性的計畫 , 二十美元給男性的計劃 。
women are 51 percent of humankind .	女性是51%的人 。
empowering them will change everything more than technology and design and entertainment .	賦予他們能改變一切 , 不只是科技、設計和娛樂 。
i can promise you that women working together linked , informed and educated can bring peace and prosperity to this forsaken planet .	我可以保證各位 , 女性一起工作 , 結合起來 , 受教育 , 和平和平繁榮 , 能夠為此受惠 。
in any war today , most of the casualties are civilians , mainly women and children . they are collateral damage .	在今天的戰爭中 , 大部分的戰爭都是公民 , 主要是女性和小孩 , 主要是婦女和小孩 。
men run the world , and look at the mess we have .	男人經營世界 , 看看我們有的混亂 。
what kind of world do we want ?	我們想要什麼樣的世界 ?
this is a fundamental question that most of us are asking .	我們大部分人都在問這個問題 。
does it make sense to participate in the existing world order ?	是否合理參與現存的世界秩序 ?
we want a world where life is preserved and the quality of life is enriched for everybody , not only for the privileged .	我們想要一個世界 , 生活的品質是為每個人 , 不只是為了榮幸 。
in january i saw an exhibit of fernando botero's paintings at the uc berkeley library .	在一月 , 我看到了費倫多•波特羅的畫畫在柏克萊圖書館 。
no museum or gallery in the united states , except for the new york gallery that carries botero's work , has dared to show the paintings because the theme is the abu ghraib prison .	在美國 , 沒有博物館或ghraib監獄 , 除了在紐約市區的藝術家裡 , 展示了畫作 , 因為主題是阿布•卡里斯 。
they are huge paintings of torture and abuse of power , in the voluminous botero style .	他們是很大的畫作和濫用權力 , 在廣大的畫作中 , 被強暴的虐待和濫用 。
i have not been able to get those images out of my mind or my heart .	我無法從我的腦袋或心中得到這些影像 。
what i fear most is power with impunity .	我害怕大部分的力量是權力 。
i fear abuse of power , and the power to abuse .	我害怕濫用權力 , 權力濫用權力 。
in our species , the alpha males define reality , and force the rest of the pack to accept that reality and follow the rules .	在我們的物種中 , 雄性領袖定義現實 , 並遵守規則 。
the rules change all the time , but they always benefit them , and in this case , the trickledown effect , which does not work in economics , works perfectly .	規則改變了所有時間 , 但他們總是對他們有益處 , 尤其是在經濟學上 , 這種情況下 , 效果不在於經濟上運作得很完美 。
abuse trickles down from the top of the ladder to the bottom .	下層的層面下降到底層 。
women and children , especially the poor , are at the bottom .	女性和孩子 , 特別是貧窮 , 尤其是窮人 。
even the most destitute of men have someone they can abuse a woman or a child .	即使是最高層的婦女還是小孩 , 她們可以虐待女性或小孩 。
i'm fed up with the power that a few exert over the many through gender , income , race , and class .	我在許多性別、收入、種族和課堂上都得到了許多性別的權力 。
i think that the time is ripe to make fundamental changes in our civilization .	我認為 , 時間在我們的文明中創造基礎的改變 。
but for real change , we need feminine energy in the management of the world .	但 , 為了真正的改變 , 我們需要女性能源在全世界的管理 。
we need a critical number of women in positions of power , and we need to nurture the feminine energy in men .	我們需要培養女性權力的女性權力 , 我們需要培養女性的權力 。
i'm talking about men with young minds , of course .	當然 , 我在談男人和年輕人 , 當然 。
old guys are hopeless ; we have to wait for them to die off .	老舊人無希望 ; 我們等待他們死掉 。
yes , i would love to have sophia loren's long legs and legendary breasts .	是的 , 我很喜歡有蘇菲亞•洛倫的長腿和腿部 。
but given a choice , i would rather have the warrior hearts of wangari maathai , somaly mam , jenny and rose mapendo .	但 , 為了選擇 , 我寧願是瑪麗•瑪麗馬的母親 , 珍妮和羅斯地圖 。
i want to make this world good .	我想要讓這個世界變得更好 。
not better , but to make it good .	不是更好的 , 但要讓它好好 。
why not ? it is possible . look around in this room all this knowledge , energy , talent and technology .	為何不呢 ? 看看這個房間所有的知識、能源、天才和科技 。
let's get off our fannies , roll up our sleeves and get to work , passionately , in creating an almost perfect world .	咱們脫離我們的粉絲 , 打開我們的美麗 , 創造出完美的世界 。
every day , in a city the size of london , 30 million meals are served . but where does all the food come from ? architect carolyn steel discusses the daily miracle of feeding a city , and shows how ancient food routes shaped the modern world .	每天 , 每一天 , 在城市裡 , 有300萬美金的食物都被服務 , 但從哪裡來的 ? 建築師卡羅•史黛爾提到 , 現代世界有多麼的不可思議 。
cities , culture , food , global issues	城市、文化、食物、全球議題 。
carolyn steel: how food shapes our cities	卡羅琳•史蒂:我們城市如何塑造我們的城市 。
how do you feed a city ?	你要如何餵飽城市 ?
it's one of the great questions of our time .	這是我們時代最大的問題之一 。
yet it's one that's rarely asked .	但 , 很少人會被問到 。
we take it for granted that if we go into a shop or restaurant , or indeed into this theater's foyer in about an hour's time , there is going to be food there waiting for us , having magically come from somewhere .	我們認真思考 , 如果我們進入一間餐廳 , 或餐廳 , 或餐廳 , 或餐廳 , 或餐廳 , 或餐廳 , 或餐廳 , 即將進入一家餐廳 , 到一間餐廳 , 到一間餐廳 , 到一間房間的餐廳 , 隨之而來 。
but when you think that every day for a city the size of london , enough food has to be produced , transported , bought and sold , cooked , eaten , disposed of , and that something similar has to happen every day for every city on earth , it's remarkable that cities get fed at all .	但當你認為每一天城市都市大小的倫敦 , 都可以被運輸、買賣、煮飯、吃、被吃掉、被交通 , 被用來製造、被運輸、買賣、煮飯、吃掉 , 和被賣掉的食物 , 會被運輸 , 買賣、煮飯、吃掉 , 被用來製造 , 被賣掉 , 被賣掉 。
we live in places like this as if they're the most natural things in the world , forgetting that because we're animals and that we need to eat , we're actually as dependent on the natural world as our ancient ancestors were .	我們生活在這個世界裡 , 如同我們所居住的自然世界一樣 , 儘管我們是人類的祖先 , 卻依賴自然界的天然 , 我們依賴自然世界 , 以我們的古老祖先生存 。
and as more of us move into cities , more of that natural world is being transformed into extraordinary landscapes like the one behind me it's soybean fields in mato grosso in brazil in order to feed us .	隨著我們搬進城市裡 , 大自然世界被轉變成非凡的景色 , 像是我在巴西的大草原 , 來餵飽我們 。
these are extraordinary landscapes , but few of us ever get to see them .	這些是非凡的地景 , 但少數人會看到它們 。
and increasingly these landscapes are not just feeding us either .	越來越多的地景並不只是餵飽我們 。
as more of us move into cities , more of us are eating meat , so that a third of the annual grain crop globally now gets fed to animals rather than to us human animals .	搬進城市裡 , 更多人吃肉 , 所以 , 現今全世界的三分之一的穀物被餵養動物 , 而不是人類的動物 。
and given that it takes three times as much grain actually ten times as much grain to feed a human if it's passed through an animal first , that's not a very efficient way of feeding us .	若有三倍的穀物能餵飽人類 , 那就不是很有效的方法 , 餵飽我們 。
and it's an escalating problem too .	這也是一個嚴重的問題 。
by 2050 , it's estimated that twice the number of us are going to be living in cities .	到了2050年 , 估計我們將要活在城市裡的人口數量 。
and it's also estimated that there is going to be twice as much meat and dairy consumed .	同時也估計 , 兩倍的肉類和大量的肉類都消耗了 。
so meat and urbanism are rising hand in hand .	所以 , 肉和都市主義正在舉手 。
and that's going to pose an enormous problem .	這將會帶來一個巨大的問題 。
six billion hungry carnivores to feed , by 2050 .	六十億個飢餓的糖果在2050年 。
that's a big problem . and actually if we carry on as we are , it's a problem we're very unlikely to be able to solve .	這是個很大的問題 。 事實上如果我們帶著這問題 , 我們就很難解決 。
nineteen million hectares of rainforest are lost every year to create new arable land .	每年有九千萬公頃的雨林 , 創造出新的可耕地 。
although at the same time we're losing an equivalent amount of existing arables to salinization and erosion .	雖然同時 , 我們也失去了一份相當量的存在性 , 用來清除和暴露 。
we're very hungry for fossil fuels too .	我們對化石燃料也很感興趣 。
it takes about 10 calories to produce every calorie of food that we consume in the west .	要花大約10卡路里 , 才能製造出我們在西方所消耗的食物 。
and even though there is food that we are producing at great cost , we don't actually value it .	儘管我們有食物在大成本上 , 我們並不珍視它 。
half the food produced in the usa is currently thrown away .	美國目前有一半的食物被丟棄 。
and to end all of this , at the end of this long process , we're not even managing to feed the planet properly .	要結束這段漫長的過程 , 我們還沒辦法餵飽地球 。
a billion of us are obese , while a further billion starve .	我們有十億人是肥胖者 , 十億人是肥胖 。
none of it makes very much sense .	這一點都不合理 。
and when you think that 80 percent of global trade in food now is controlled by just five multinational corporations , it's a grim picture .	當你認為百分之八十的全球交易已經被五個跨國公司所控制 , 它是一張圖片 。
as we're moving into cities , the world is also embracing a western diet .	當我們搬進城市時 , 世界也擁抱了西方飲食 。
and if we look to the future , it's an unsustainable diet .	如果我們看看未來 , 它是一個不可持續的飲食 。
so how did we get here ?	我們是怎麼做到的 ?
and more importantly , what are we going to do about it ?	更重要的是 , 我們要怎麼做 ?
well , to answer the slightly easier question first , about 10 , 000 years ago , i would say , is the beginning of this process in the ancient near east , known as the fertile crescent .	首先 , 要回答一些簡單的問題 , 大約一萬年前 , 我會說 , 這是在古老的早期 , 叫做 「 肥沃克里斯 」 。
because , as you can see , it was crescent shaped .	因為 , 如你所見 , 它是被設計的 。
and it was also fertile .	同時也是肥沃 。
and it was here , about 10 , 000 years ago , that two extraordinary inventions , agriculture and urbanism , happened roughly in the same place and at the same time .	大約一萬年前 , 這兩個非凡的發明 , 農業和城市主義 , 發生在同一個地方 , 同時也發生了 。
this is no accident , because agriculture and cities are bound together . they need each other .	這不是意外 , 因為農業和城市都互相合作 。 他們需要彼此 。
because it was discovery of grain by our ancient ancestors for the first time that produced a food source that was large enough and stable enough to support permanent settlements .	由於古老祖先第一次製造出食物來源 , 足以支撐永久的住宅 。
and if we look at what those settlements were like , we see they were compact .	如果我們看看這些組成的樣子 , 我們會看到它們是比較的 。
they were surrounded by productive farm land and dominated by large temple complexes like this one at ur , that were , in fact , effectively , spiritualized , central food distribution centers .	他們被生產力的農場所組成 , 中央食物分配中心 , 中央食物分配中心 。
because it was the temples that organized the harvest , gathered in the grain , offered it to the gods , and then offered the grain that the gods didn't eat back to the people .	因為它是神聖經營的寺廟 , 把穀物帶給上帝 , 然後提供給上帝的神 , 再給上帝 , 再給上帝們 。
so , if you like , the whole spiritual and physical life of these cities was dominated by the grain and the harvest that sustained them .	所以 , 如果你喜歡 , 所有這些城市的靈性和實體生活都是由穀物和穀物所組成的 。
and in fact , that's true of every ancient city .	事實上 , 每個古老的城市都一樣 。
but of course not all of them were that small .	但當然不是所有人都很小 。
famously , rome had about a million citizens by the first century a . d .	很有名的 , 羅馬有一百萬個市民 , 由第一世紀的主題 。
so how did a city like this feed itself ?	那麼 , 這種城市如何像這樣的城市這樣做 ?
the answer is what i call " ancient food miles . "	答案是 , 我稱之為 「 古代食物英哩 」 。
basically , rome had access to the sea , which made it possible for it to import food from a very long way away .	基本上 , 羅馬接觸了海洋 , 讓它可以從遠遠的路途中取得海洋 。
this is the only way it was possible to do this in the ancient world , because it was very difficult to transport food over roads , which were rough .	這是在古代世界的唯一方法 , 因為它很難交通運輸食物 , 路上也很困難 。
and the food obviously went off very quickly .	食物顯然很快 。
so rome effectively waged war on places like carthage and egypt just to get its paws on their grain reserves .	所以 , 羅馬有效的戰爭 , 像是卡和埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及埃及
and , in fact , you could say that the expansion of the empire was really sort of one long , drawn out militarized shopping spree , really .	事實上 , 你可以說 , 擴張帝國的擴張 , 其實是很長的一段漫畫 , 以軍事化購物的擴張 。
in fact i love the fact , i just have to mention this: rome in fact used to import oysters from london , at one stage . i think that's extraordinary .	事實上 , 我真的很喜歡這個事實:羅馬被用於倫敦的博士館裡 , 一個階段 , 我覺得這很奇特 。
so rome shaped its hinterland through its appetite .	所以羅馬形塑了它的希臘風格 , 用它的形狀 。
but the interesting thing is that the other thing also happened in the preindustrial world .	但有趣的是 , 另一件事也發生在工業世界 。
if we look at a map of london in the 17th century , we can see that its grain , which is coming in from the thames , along the bottom of this map .	如果我們看看倫敦的地圖的地圖 , 我們可以看到它的地圖是從十七世紀開始的地圖的地圖 , 我們可以看到它的地圖 。
so the grain markets were to the south of the city .	所以 , 葡萄酒是城市的南方 。
and the roads leading up from them to cheapside , which was the main market , were also grain markets .	道路從他們到便宜的道路 , 主要市場 , 也是穀物市場 。
and if you look at the name of one of those streets , bread street , you can tell what was going on there 300 years ago .	如果你看看那些街頭的名字 , 可以告訴你在300年前發生了什麼 。
and the same of course was true for fish .	魚類也是如此 。
fish was , of course , coming in by river as well . same thing .	當然 , 魚類也在河流裡 , 也是一樣的 。
and of course billingsgate , famously , was london's fish market , operating onsite here until the mid1980s .	當然 , 很有名的是倫敦的魚市場 , 在1980年代中期 。
which is extraordinary , really , when you think about it .	這很不可思議 , 真的 , 當你想到它的時候 。
everybody else was wandering around with mobile phones that looked like bricks and sort of smelly fish happening down on the port .	每個人都在移動電話裡 , 像磚塊一樣 , 像磚塊一樣 , 在港口附近 。
this is another thing about food in cities: once its roots into the city are established , they very rarely move .	這也是關於食物的另一件事:一旦它根源到城市中 , 它們非常少移動 。
meat is a very different story because , of course , animals could walk into the city .	肉是一種非常不同的故事因為當然 , 動物可以走進城市
so much of london's meat was coming from the northwest , from scotland and wales .	很多倫敦的肉來自來自蘇格蘭和威爾斯
so it was coming in , and arriving at the city at the northwest , which is why smithfield , london's very famous meat market , was located up there .	所以 , 來到這裡 , 來到北方的冰山 , 那裡是為smithfield , 倫敦的一座非常有名的肉市場 , 在那裡 。
poultry was coming in from east anglia and so on , to the northeast .	來自東加利亞 , 到東北方 , 到東部 。
i feel a bit like a weather woman doing this . anyway , and so the birds were coming in with their feet protected with little canvas shoes .	我覺得有點像天氣女性 , 這樣做 , 鳥兒們就來到他們的腳邊 , 用雙腳來保護小小的羽毛 。
and then when they hit the eastern end of cheapside , that's where they were sold , which is why it's called poultry .	然後當他們打到東方時 , 那裡被賣掉了 , 那裡是被賣出來的 , 這就是為何被賣出來的 。
and , in fact , if you look at the map of any city built before the industrial age , you can trace food coming in to it .	事實上 , 如果你看一下在工業時代的地圖 , 你就能收到食物來源 。
you can actually see how it was physically shaped by food , both by reading the names of the streets , which give you a lot of clues .	你可以看到它是如何形狀的 , 透過食物 , 讀了街道的名字 , 給你很多線索 。
friday street , in a previous life , is where you went to buy your fish on a friday .	星期五街道 , 在一個早期的人生中 , 你去買你的魚 , 去買你的魚 。
but also you have to imagine it full of food .	但你必須想像一下它充滿了食物 。
because the streets and the public spaces were the only places where food was bought and sold .	因為街道和公共空間只是食物被買賣的唯一地方 。
and if we look at an image of smithfield in 1830 you can see that it would have been very difficult to live in a city like this and be unaware of where your food came from .	如果我們看一下史密斯密斯密斯密斯密斯密斯密斯密斯密斯密斯密斯密斯密斯密斯密斯密斯密斯密斯密斯密斯密斯密斯的照片 , 你可以看到它會很難生活在這個城市裡 , 不管你是怎麼辦到的 。
in fact , if you were having sunday lunch , the chances were it was mooing or bleating outside your window about three days earlier .	事實上 , 如果你有陽日午餐 , 機會是在你的窗戶外面打開 , 一天午餐 , 機會就在你的窗戶外面三天 。
so this was obviously an organic city , part of an organic cycle .	這很明顯是有機循環的一部分 。
and then 10 years later everything changed .	十年後 , 一切改變了 。
this is an image of the great western in 1840 .	這是1840年大西方的圖片 。
and as you can see , some of the earliest train passengers were pigs and sheep .	你們可以看到 , 最早的訓練乘客是豬和羊 。
so all of a sudden , these animals are no longer walking into market .	突然間 , 這些動物不再走進市場 。
they're being slaughtered out of sight and mind , somewhere in the countryside .	他們被屠殺 , 不管是在鄉村裡的任何地方 。
and they're coming into the city by rail .	後來他們進入城市裡 ,
and this changes everything .	這改變了一切 。
to start off with , it makes it possible for the first time to grow cities , really any size and shape , in any place .	首先 , 要從事開始 , 首次要成長城市 , 大小和形狀 , 任何地方都有可能 。
cities used to be constrained by geography ; they used to have to get their food through very difficult physical means .	城市以前被地理所限制 , 他們習慣要把食物帶到非常困難的實體上 。
all of a sudden they are effectively emancipated from geography .	突然間 , 他們都有效地理由地理 。
and as you can see from these maps of london , in the 90 years after the trains came , it goes from being a little blob that was quite easy to feed by animals coming in on foot , and so on , to a large splurge , that would be very , very difficult to feed with anybody on foot , either animals or people .	如你所見 , 從倫敦的地圖上 , 到九十年後 , 在火車後 , 一個大型的運輸 , 會非常非常困難 , 要餵飽任何人 , 不論是動物或人 , 都很容易 。
and of course that was just the beginning . after the trains came cars , and really this marks the end of this process .	當然那只是一開始 , 火車結束了 。 火車結束了這個過程 。
it's the final emancipation of the city from any apparent relationship with nature at all .	它是整個城市的最後一個與大自然的聯繫 。
and this is the kind of city that's devoid of smell , devoid of mess , certainly devoid of people , because nobody would have dreamed of walking in such a landscape .	這種城市 , 沒有人會夢想在這樣的地景上走動 , 沒有人會夢想著那樣的城市 。
in fact , what they did to get food was they got in their cars , drove to a box somewhere on the outskirts , came back with a week's worth of shopping , and wondered what on earth to do with it .	事實上 , 他們的食物是他們買的 , 拿到箱子裡 , 一週的購物 , 買到箱子裡 , 想知道地球上有哪些東西 。
and this really is the moment when our relationship , both with food and cities , changes completely .	這真的是我們的關係 , 食物和城市的改變 , 完全改變了 。
here we have food that used to be the center , the social core of the city at the periphery .	這裡我們有食物曾經是城市的中心 , 城市的核心 , 城市的核心 。
it used to be a social event , buying and selling food .	以前是社交活動 , 買賣食物 。
we used to cook ; now we just add water , or a little bit of an egg if you're making a cake or something .	我們以前會煮飯 , 只要加入水 , 或一些蛋糕 , 或一些蛋 。
we don't smell food to see if it's okay to eat .	我們不會聞到食物來看看是否好吃 。
we just read the back of a label on a packet .	我們只是在一頭包裝上標記 。
and we don't value food . we don't trust it .	我們沒有價值食物 , 我們不信任它 。
so instead of trusting it , we fear it .	所以 , 我們不相信它 , 我們害怕它 。
and instead of valuing it , we throw it away .	而不是評估它 , 我們把它丟掉 。
one of the great ironies of modern food systems is that they've made the very thing they promised to make easier much harder .	現代食物系統最棒的諷刺之一就是他們承諾要做得更容易 。
by making it possible to build cities anywhere and any place , they've actually distanced us from our most important relationship , which is that of us and nature .	只要讓它能夠建造城市 , 任何地方 , 它們都能在我們和大自然中建立城市 。
and also they've made us dependent on systems that only they can deliver , that , as we've seen , are unsustainable .	同時 , 它們也讓我們依賴系統 , 只能提供我們所見 , 不穩定的系統 。
so what are we going to do about that ?	那麼 , 我們要怎麼做呢 ?
it's not a new question .	這不是一個新問題 。
500 years ago it's what thomas more was asking himself .	500年前 , 湯瑪斯會問自己自己 。
this is the frontispiece of his book " utopia . "	這是他的書《烏托邦》 。
and it was a series of semiindependent citystates , if that sounds remotely familiar , a day's walk from one another where everyone was basically farmingmad , and grew vegetables in their back gardens , and ate communal meals together , and so on .	這是一系列獨立的公共餐廳 , 每人都很熟悉 , 每天都能從另一邊走出 , 一邊是一家餐廳 , 和餐廳裡的餐廳 , 和餐廳的餐廳 , 再來交流 。
and i think you could argue that food is a fundamental ordering principle of utopia , even though more never framed it that way .	我想你可以說食物是烏托邦的基本原則 , 儘管它不是如此 。
and here is another very famous " utopian " vision , that of ebenezer howard , " the garden city . "	還有另一個非常有名的烏托邦 「 烏托邦 」 視覺 , 叫做烏托邦 " 烏托邦 " 的名字 " 烏托邦 " 的名字 " 烏托邦 " 的名字 " 烏托邦 "
same idea: series of semiindependent citystates , little blobs of metropolitan stuff with arable land around , joined to one another by railway .	同一個想法:一系列獨立的城市 , 一間小型的土地 , 由鐵路運送 , 再加入到另一條鐵路 。
and again , food could be said to be the ordering principle of his vision .	再次 , 食物可以被說是他的視野的原則 。
it even got built , but nothing to do with this vision that howard had .	它甚至被建造了 , 但和這個願景相比 , 沒什麼關係 。
and that is the problem with these utopian ideas , that they are utopian .	這些烏托邦的想法是烏托邦的問題 ,
utopia was actually a word that thomas moore used deliberately .	烏托邦其實是thomasmoore使用的詞 。
it was a kind of joke , because it's got a double derivation from the greek .	這是個笑話 , 因為它有來自希臘的二氧化碳 。
it can either mean a good place , or no place .	它可以說是好地方 , 或沒有地方 。
because it's an ideal . it's an imaginary thing . we can't have it .	因為這是一個理想的 , 一個理想的 , 這是個理想的 。 這是個理想的 。
and i think , as a conceptual tool for thinking about the very deep problem of human dwelling , that makes it not much use .	我認為 , 作為一個概念性的工具 , 來思考人類的深層問題 , 會讓它不用用 。
so i've come up with an alternative , which is sitopia , from the ancient greek , " sitos " for food , and " topos " for place .	所以 , 我得到了一個替代方案 , 叫做 「 stopia 」 , 從古希臘、 「 stopia 」 、 「 stos 」 到 「 stopia 」 。
i believe we already live in sitopia .	我相信我們已經住在烏托邦 。
we live in a world shaped by food , and if we realize that , we can use food as a really powerful tool a conceptual tool , design tool , to shape the world differently .	我們生活在世界各地 , 如果我們意識到 , 我們能用食物來形塑這個世界 , 更有用的工具 , 設計工具 , 來塑造世界不同 。
so if we were to do that , what might sitopia look like ?	所以 , 如果我們要這麼做 , 烏托邦看起來是什麼樣子 ?
well i think it looks a bit like this .	我覺得它看起來有點像這樣 。
i have to use this slide . it's just the look on the face of the dog .	我必須用這張投影片 , 看看狗的臉 。
but anyway , this is it's food at the center of life , at the center of family life , being celebrated , being enjoyed , people taking time for it .	不管怎樣 , 這是食物在生活的中心 , 家庭生活的中心 , 被讚頌 , 享受 , 人們花時間 。
this is where food should be in our society .	食物應該在我們的社會中 。
but you can't have scenes like this unless you have people like this .	但你不能像這樣的景象 , 除非你有這樣的人 。
by the way , these can be men as well .	順便一提 , 這些人也能成為男人 。
it's people who think about food , who think ahead , who plan , who can stare at a pile of raw vegetables and actually recognize them .	人們會想到食物 , 想到食物的人 , 想知道 , 誰會想食物 , 誰會想食物 , 誰會想食物 , 誰會想著食物 ?
we need these people . we're part of a network .	我們需要這些人 , 我們是網路的一部分 。
because without these kinds of people we can't have places like this .	因為沒有這些我們無法擁有這樣的人 。
here , i deliberately chose this because it is a man buying a vegetable .	在這裡 , 我輕鬆地選擇這個 , 因為那是男人買蔬菜 。
but networks , markets where food is being grown locally .	但網絡 , 市場 , 食物正在成長的地方 。
it's common . it's fresh .	它很普遍 , 很常見 。
it's part of the social life of the city .	它是社會生活的一部分 。
because without that , you can't have this kind of place , food that is grown locally and also is part of the landscape , and is not just a zerosum commodity off in some unseen hellhole .	因為 , 沒有這種地方 , 你不能有這種地方 , 食物是地景的一部分 , 而不是僅僅零和零的產業 , 不再只是零件商品 。
cows with a view .	牛和觀點相同 。
steaming piles of humus .	蒸汽的山脈 。
this is basically bringing the whole thing together .	這基本上就是把整整組合在一起 。
and this is a community project i visited recently in toronto .	這是我最近參加的社區計劃 。
it's a greenhouse , where kids get told all about food and growing their own food .	這是溫室 , 孩子們被告知食物的食物 , 和培養自己的食物 。
here is a plant called kevin , or maybe it's a plant belonging to a kid called kevin . i don't know .	這裡有一個叫做kevin的植物 , 或者它是一個植物屬於一個叫做kevin的植物 , 我不知道 。
but anyway , these kinds of projects that are trying to reconnect us with nature is extremely important .	總之 , 這些計畫正在試圖重新連結我們大自然是極為重要的 。
so sitopia , for me , is really a way of seeing .	所以 , 西托比亞 , 對我而言 , 這是一種看法 。
it's basically recognizing that sitopia already exists in little pockets everywhere .	基本上 , 蜜蜂已經存在於小小的口袋裡 。
the trick is to join them up , to use food as a way of seeing .	技巧是要加入他們 , 用食物來當作一種看法 。
and if we do that , we're going to stop seeing cities as big , metropolitan , unproductive blobs , like this .	如果我們這樣做 , 我們就會停止看到城市 , 像這樣 , 大型的城市 , 像這樣 。
we're going to see them more like this , as part of the productive , organic framework of which they are inevitably a part , symbiotically connected .	我們會把它們視為是有機架構的一部分 , 它們是無可避免地連結在一起的一部分 。
but of course , that's not a great image either , because we need not to be producing food like this anymore .	當然 , 這不是很棒的圖像 , 因為我們不需要再把食物做成 。
we need to be thinking more about permaculture , which is why i think this image just sums up for me the kind of thinking we need to be doing .	我們需要思考更多關於永生性 , 這就是為什麼我認為這張圖像只是為了我認為這張圖只是為了我們要做的事 。
it's a reconceptualization of the way food shapes our lives .	它是一種重新思考食物形塑我們的生活方式 。
the best image i know of this is from 650 years ago .	我所知道的最好的圖像是650年前 。
it's ambrogio lorenzetti's " allegory of good government . "	亞伯羅•洛倫澤蒂的 「 都是好的政府 」 。
it's about the relationship between the city and the countryside .	它是關於城市和國家之間的關係 。
and i think the message of this is very clear .	我認為這訊息很明顯 。
if the city looks after the country , the country will look after the city .	如果城市看了這個國家 , 國家就會看這個城市 。
and i want us to ask now , what would ambrogio lorenzetti paint if he painted this image today ?	現在我要請大家問 , 如果他畫畫這張圖 , 阿布羅吉歐•洛倫澤蒂畫了什麼 ?
what would an allegory of good government look like today ?	現今的政府長大 , 什麼是好的 ?
because i think it's an urgent question .	因為我認為這是一個迫切的問題 。
it's one we have to ask , and we have to start answering .	我們必須問 , 我們必須開始回答 。
we know we are what we eat .	我們知道我們是吃的 。
we need to realize that the world is also what we eat .	我們必須了解 , 世界也是我們吃的 。
but if we take that idea , we can use food as a really powerful tool to shape the world better .	但如果我們採用這個概念 , 我們可以用食物作為一個非常強大的工具 , 來塑造世界更好 。
weeks from the charter for compassion launch , karen armstrong looks at religion's role in the 21st century: will its dogmas divide us ? or will it unite us for common good ? she reviews the catalysts that can drive the world's faiths to rediscover the golden rule .	幾週後 , 卡爾德•阿姆斯壯觀看宗教的角色在21世紀:它會否認我們同情心 , 卡爾斯壯觀看宗教的角色在21世紀:它會否認同理心的主題 ? 或將它帶給我們共同的好處 ? 她重新審視了宗教的角色在21世紀:它會讓世界的信仰轉變 , 來重新審視宗教的角色 。
god , ted prize , global issues , politics , religion , tedglobal2009 , violence	上帝 , tedprize , 全球議題 , 政治 , 宗教 , tedprize , 全球議題 , 政治 , 宗教 , 2009年 , 暴力 。
karen armstrong: let's revive the golden rule	karenemstrong:讓我們保證黃金法則 。
for years i've been feeling frustrated , because as a religious historian , i've become acutely aware of the centrality of compassion in all the major world faiths .	多年來 , 我變得很沮喪 , 因為身為宗教歷史學家 , 我變得很沮喪 , 因為當宗教歷史學家 , 我變得很挫折 , 因為身為宗教歷史學家 , 我變得很挫折 , 因為身為宗教歷史學家 , 我變得很沮喪 。
every single one of them has evolved their own version of what's been called the golden rule .	每一個人都演化出自己的版本 , 叫做黃金法則 。
sometimes it comes in a positive version " always treat all others as you'd like to be treated yourself . "	有時候 , 正面的版本是 「 總是對待你自己 。 」
and equally important is the negative version " don't do to others what you would not like them to do to you . "	同樣重要的是負面版本: 「 不要對其他人做你不喜歡他們做的事 。 」
look into your own heart , discover what it is that gives you pain and then refuse , under any circumstance whatsoever , to inflict that pain on anybody else .	看看你的心臟 , 發現它是什麼讓你痛苦 , 然後拒絕 , 在任何情況下 , 在任何情況下 , 都能讓你痛苦 , 然後拒絕 , 在任何情況下 , 都能讓你痛苦 。
and people have emphasized the importance of compassion , not just because it sounds good , but because it works .	人們強調了同情心的重要性 , 不只是因為它聽起來很好 , 而是因為它是好的 。

the stucco on the walls of most of the buildings in rome covers the scars ; the scars of centuries of change as these structures have been adapted rather than being torn down .	羅馬大樓的牆壁上大部分的建築物都被綁架了 , 數百年以來都被改造 , 而不是被灌輸 。

" pigeon's progress " struck me as a catchy title .	「 鴿子進步 」 讓我變成了 「 鴿子的進步 」 。
if it was a homing pigeon , it would be called " homer's odyssey . "	如果它是一名叫做 「 家的奧德修斯 」 的名字 。
but it was the journey of the . . .	但它是這段旅程 。
i mean , if a title works , use it . but it would be a journey that went through rome and showed all the things that i like about rome .	我的意思是 , 如果一個標題 , 可以用它 , 但它會是個旅程 , 穿越羅馬的旅程 , 用它來呈現我所喜歡的羅馬 。
it's a pigeon sitting on top of a church .	這是一隻鴿子坐在教堂上 。
goes off during the day and does normal pigeon stuff . comes back , the whole place is covered with scaffolding and green netting and there's no way this pigeon can get home .	在日常的鴿子回來的時候 , 整個地方都被捕撈、綠色和綠色包裹著 , 完全沒有鴿子可以回家 。
so it's a homeless pigeon now and it's going to have to find another place to live , and that allows me to go through my catalog of favorite things , and we start with the tall ones and so on .	所以這是一隻無家可歸的旅鴿 , 牠必須找到另一個地方居住的地方 , 讓我可以從我最喜歡的物品開始 , 到那裡 , 牠會找到另一個地方 。
maybe it has to go back and live with family members ; that's not always a good thing , but it does sort of bring pigeons together again .	也許牠必須回到家族成員身上 , 不一定是好事 , 但它會帶鴿子回來 。
and i thought , that's sort of interesting , but maybe there's a person who should be involved in this in some way .	我覺得這很有趣 , 但也許有一個人應該參與其中 。
so i kind of came up with this old guy who spends his life looking after sick pigeons .	所以我想出了這個老傢伙 , 他花了他的生命在追蹤鴿子 。

in the old roman custom , the dead were never buried within the walls .	在古羅馬的經營中 , 死人從未埋藏在牆壁中 。

. that's really going to go a long way .	這真的很長一段時間 。
so anyway , i went through . . . and again , if packaging doesn't work and if the stories aren't going anywhere , i just come up with titles and hope that a title will sort of kick me off in the right direction .	不管怎樣 , 我就不去了 , 如果包裝不在正確的方向上 , 我就在正確的方向前 , 把我拉到右邊的方向 。

past the pyramid of cestius these will seem very familiar to you , even if you haven't been to rome recently past the gatehouse .	過去的金字塔基金字塔看起來很熟悉 , 即使你以前也不是羅馬最近被送到gatehe 。

and then bird manages to pull itself together past this medieval tower one of the few remaining medieval towers towards the church of sant'agnese and around the dome looking down into piazza navona which we've already mentioned and seen and flown over a couple of times ; there's the bernini statue of the four rivers and then past the wonderful borromini sant'ivo , stopping just long enough on the 26foot diameter oculus of the pantheon to catch our breath .	接著 , 鳥類管理會把它們帶到一邊最好的巴黎明尼河 , 穿越了美麗的巴西尼尼雕像 , 四河流過來 , 直到我們剛剛提到的 , 漫長在26英尺深的直徑上 , 穿越了美麗的巴西尼尼雕像 , 四河流過來 , 最後又有了美麗的貝尼尼雕像 , 穿越了美麗的巴西尼尼雕像 , 四河流過來 , 直到我們剛剛提到 , 停止足夠久以26英尺深的直徑 。
and then we can swoop inside and around ; and because we're flying , we don't really have to worry about gravity at this particular moment in time , so this drawing can be oriented in any way on the page .	然後我們就在飛行 , 我們不需要擔心重力在哪裡 , 所以這張圖片可以隨時隨地產生 。
we get a little exuberant as we pass gesu ; it's not surprising to sort of mimic the architecture in this way .	當我們通過gesu時 , 它並不意外會模仿這個建築 。
past the wonderful wall filled with the juxtaposition that i was talking about ; beautiful carvings set into the walls above the neon " ristorante " sign , and so on .	美妙的牆壁上滿滿了我剛剛談過的美麗的牆壁 , 被稱為 「 監獄 」 的標誌 , 同時也出現了 。
